The following is an index of each JSON property used in the [JSON format](https://github.com/usnistgov/OSCAL/blob/v1.0.1/json/schema/oscal_ssp_schema.json) for this [model](/concepts/layer/implementation/ssp/). Each entry in the index lists all uses of the given property in the format, which is linked to the corresponding entry in the [JSON Format Reference](../json-reference/). Each entry also lists the formal name for the definition which is linked to the corresponding JSON definition in the [JSON Format Metaschema Reference](../json-definitions/).

   <section class="named-object-group">
      <h1 class="toc1" id="/responsibilities">responsibilities</h1>
